Anonymous ID:Pn4l9I6r Mon 08 Apr 2024 17:39:56 No.464381335  ViewReport
>>464379926
Zeus, deus, deiwós, di̯ḗus, *dei, Doublet of dīvus; related to Iūpiter, Jupiter. All relating to shining sky father. So what does this have to do with Odin? The older form of his name is pronounced Wotan or Wodan.

The Latin vates - noun, masculine - means 'seer, prophet'. The cognate in Irish is 'fāith', where the 'v' became an 'f' as it normally does in Gaelic. The Celtic word is highly likely to have been close to the Latin.

Pokorny states: Anglo-Saxon - Wōden - (prop. n. masc) is given as a reflex (a cognate) for 'vates'.

From Etymonline: god. Old English god, 'supreme being, deity', from proto-Germanic *guthan (cf. Du. 'god', German 'Gott', Old Norse 'guð', Goth 'guþ'), from proto-Indo-European *ghut - 'that which is invoked' (cf. Skt. huta - 'invoked', an epithet of Indra), from the root *gheu(e) - 'to call, invoke'. This seems to be a related word.

From the Proto-Indo-European Etymological Dictionary by Fernando López-Menchero:
wātis = poet
wetwos = old

And quite revealingly, from the Indo-European Dictionary Translator:
qdnos = magic. (this author begs to differ with the translator, as this should begin with 'qw' or 'kw', then a vowel, then '-dnos'.)

One has to wonder if Wotan was not a name, but instead a title or job description, 'diviner' and 'magician'. The proposition here is that this is exactly what it was. So how did this become a deity? So if Jesus is King of Kings who honors his father. Wotan is the ALL FATHER

The document reflects on the contemporary understanding of human dignity, particularly in the context of the 1948 United Nations Declaration of Human Rights. It emphasizes that human dignity is intrinsic to the person, not granted or revoked by others based on external factors. This intrinsic dignity forms the basis for human rights and is recognized universally. It acknowledges the growing awareness of human dignity in contemporary society and emphasizes its universality and inviolability. It provides a robust framework for understanding and promoting human dignity in an increasingly complex and interconnected world.

The document affirms the equal dignity of all individuals, rooted in the belief that every person is created in the image of God. This theological understanding emphasizes the intrinsic worth of every human being, irrespective of their social status, abilities, or circumstances. By grounding human dignity in the imago Dei, the document highlights the sacredness and inviolability of each person, both in body and soul.

>2. Christ Elevates Human Dignity (Paragraphs 19-21):
Building upon the foundational concept of human dignity, the document explores how the Incarnation of Christ further enhances our understanding of human worth. Through his life, teachings, and actions, Jesus affirmed the dignity of every individual, particularly those marginalized or oppressed by society. His message of love, compassion, and solidarity with the vulnerable reshaped societal attitudes towards the marginalized, inspiring acts of charity and social justice.

>Dyaus (Sanskrit: द्यौष्, IAST: Dyáuṣ) or Dyauspitr (Sanskrit: द्यौष्पितृ, IAST: Dyáuṣpitṛ́) is the Rigvedic sky deity. His consort is Prthvi, the earth goddess, and together they are the archetypal parents in the Rigveda

>Dyauṣ stems from Proto-Indo-Iranian *dyā́wš, from the Proto-Indo-European (PIE) daylight-sky god *Dyēus, and is cognate with the Greek Διας - Zeus Patēr, Illyrian Dei-pátrous, or Latin Jupiter (from Old Latin Dies piter Djous patēr), stemming from the PIE Dyḗus ph2tḗr ("Daylight-sky Father")

>The noun dyaús (when used without the pitṛ́ 'father') refers to the daylight sky, and occurs frequently in the Rigveda, as an entity. The sky in Vedic writing was described as rising in three tiers, avamá, madhyamá, and uttamá or tṛtī́ya

>Dyáuṣ Pitṛ́ appears in hymns with Prithvi Mata 'Mother Earth' in the ancient Vedic scriptures of Hinduism

>In the Ṛg·veda, Dyáuṣ Pitṛ́ appears in verses 1.89.4, 1.90.7, 1.164.33, 1.191.6, 4.1.10. and 4.17.4. He is also referred to under different theonyms: Dyavaprithvi, for example, is a dvandva compound combining 'heaven' and 'earth' as Dyauṣ and Prithvi

>Dyauṣ's most defining trait is his paternal role. His daughter, Uṣas, personifies dawn. The gods, especially Sūrya, are stated to be the children of Dyauṣ and Prithvi. Dyauṣ's other sons include Agni, Parjanya, the Ādityas, the Maruts, and the Angirases. The Ashvins are called "divó nápāt", meaning offspring/progeny/grandsons of Dyauṣ. Dyauṣ is often visualized as a roaring animal, often a bull, who fertilizes the earth

On March 21, 2024, a two-party coalition presented a draft bill to the House of Representatives (Camera dei Deputati) to protect children's privacy online and their right to their own image.

Echoing a recent French law, the proposal aims to regulate a growing digital issue known as sharenting—a contraction between share and parenting, that indicates the practice of oversharing content portraying children on social media platforms. Legislators seek to open up this debate, they said, and mitigate the security risks and psychological impacts the trend causes to youngsters.

"Totality and maximum eclipse: The Moon completely covers the disk of the Sun. Only the Sun's corona is visible. This is the most dramatic stage of a total solar eclipse. At this time, the sky goes dark, temperatures fall, and birds and animals often go quiet. The midpoint of time of totality is known as the maximum point of the eclipse."

>>463868832

The barrier to entry for game development prior to all these ready made engines being available, was actually a good thing. You had to have math aptitude, programming skill, and in many cases a passion for doing it as a hobbyist and of course, an interest in games. You didn't have to be John Carmack or Jon Blow, but there was a baseline for hiring.

But because of the scale of projects these days, studios are always looking for bodies to throw at their slop fest boondoggles, most studios will take anyone with a CS,SWE diploma or technical certification with a sparse portfolio of smaller projects. There are plenty of people with no interest in games who wind up with those certifications and also wind up working in game studios.

This is how you end up with boring slop games that have uber graphics (because assets are cheap as dirt) and are riddled with bugs. The DEI stuff is just part of the whole dumb stakeholder scheme, and makes the whole process more agonizing and alienating and just adds a patina of wokeness to these poorly engineered slop fests.
